## At a glance (read this first)

**Reevaluation (June 2026):** Normative contract in [hermes-orchestrator-local-plan.md](hermes-orchestrator-local-plan.md); **this file** is the sprint board. **Lane T (fo520–fo545)** maturity program **signed off** at **~8.5/10** — hold regressions only.

### Test health (June 2026)

**Default CI / `ci_check.ps1`:** `pytest tests -m "not integration and not slow and not benchmark"` — **~1,808 passed**, 4 skipped, **~71%** coverage on `packages/` (Streamlit `pages/**` and Maker `ui/**` omitted).

**Full tree:** run `poetry run pytest tests/` locally for integration (`-m integration`) and slow suites.

Desktop smoke uses ephemeral API port when `NIMBUSWARE_API_PORT` unset. Optional: stabilize `tests/e2e` desktop path in CI (fo541).

### What Hermes is today

Append-only Postgres events, `/v1` run lifecycle + timeline read-models, deterministic verifiers, optional Ollama preflight, bundle search + FAISS, **Postgres-backed operator config** (T1+T2 materialized; YAML export/gitops for review), Streamlit console (timeline, live critic matrix, **operator chat**, **custom agents** sidebar), **micro-slice** runs (`micro_slice` profile + automatic slice chain), **Phase 3 post-verify critic stages**, **repo-scoped retrieval memory** (`hermes_memory` + optional FAISS), **bundle usage memory**, **replay harness** (`hermes-memory-replay`), **role telemetry** + **routing suggestions** CLIs, **`scripts/install_nimbusware.py`**, and **`scripts/e2e_smoke.py`**.

**Verification:** Gates **478 passed**; full suite **2397 passed**, 19 skipped. Controller ledger is **history**, not backlog.

### Configuration store (normative §19.5 / Phase 1.5) — **core shipped**

Operator-mutable `configs/**` data **authoritatively lives in PostgreSQL** when `NIMBUSWARE_DATABASE_URL`
is set, with **materialization** into the in-memory structures orchestrator and API already use.
Optional YAML export/import for git review—not runtime dual-write.

| Tier | Migrate first | Today |
|------|----------------|-------|
| **T1** | Personas (`shelves.yaml`), roles (`roles.yaml`), workflows (`workflows/*.yaml`), frozen `policy_snapshot` at `run.created` | **Shipped (P0-a–e):** Postgres `hermes_config_document` + `ConfigMaterializer`; API/orchestrator/console write paths use store in DB mode; `policy_snapshot_from_materializer` |
| **T2** | Policy merge defaults (`model-routing.yaml` slices), escalation, integrator thresholds, self-refinement policy, `critique_pairings.yaml` | **Shipped (P0-g):** rows in `hermes_config_document`; runtime + console read via materializer in DB mode |
| **T3 (optional)** | Bundle catalog metadata | **Shipped:** Postgres read + **`GET/PUT/PATCH /v1/bundles/catalog`**; FAISS stays derived on-disk |

**Exit bar:** `run.created` freezes **`policy_snapshot`** from **materialized** config; no hot-path
`open(configs/...)` after migration for T1/T2 domains.

Full spec: [hermes-orchestrator-local-plan.md §19.5](hermes-orchestrator-local-plan.md). Implementation
backlog: [P0 — Configuration store](#p0--configuration-store-postgres-authority--materialization) below.

|------|----------|--------|

| **Lane U — User vs Admin consoles (fo310–fo317)** | **Shipped** | Maker = user console; Admin Console = admin/dev-only — [Lane U](#lane-u--user-vs-admin-consoles-fo310fo317) |
| Enterprise **OIDC / SSO** console login | Lane D polish | API-key + tenant switcher shipped (fo201/fo207); no IdP integration yet |

| Desktop E2E / `run_app` CI matrix | Optional | PZ-1 remainder; unit suite green |

## Prioritized backlog (post Phase 1.5 core + Phase C 86–90)

**Default rule:** **v1 + v2 + Phase 3 + Phase 4 + PZ are shipped** (Individual edition). New capability = **Lane M** then **Lane U** ([M build path](#lane-m--recommended-build-path), [U build path](#lane-u--recommended-build-path)). Optional: [Optional depth](#optional-depth-on-request), [Lane D polish](#lane-d--ops-polish-non-blocking), or regression fixes. Do **not** reopen YAML dual-write or §14 rows.

### P0 — Configuration store (PostgreSQL authority + materialization) — **shipped (core)**

Normative: [hermes-orchestrator-local-plan.md §19.5](hermes-orchestrator-local-plan.md), Phase **1.5**.
All slices below are **Done** in DB mode; see [Phase 1.5 shipped log](#phase-15-configuration-store-t2--gitops--persona-assignment-shipped-p0fp1).
Optional polish (`config.document.updated`, LISTEN/NOTIFY) is **P3**.

| Slice | Deliverable | Touches |
|-------|-------------|---------|
| **P0-a Schema + materializer skeleton** | Postgres tables (or `config_documents` envelope); `ConfigMaterializer` load/refresh; `NIMBUSWARE_CONFIG_FROM_DB` default-on when `NIMBUSWARE_DATABASE_URL` set | [`hermes_store/schema/postgres.sql`](packages/hermes_store/schema/postgres.sql), new `hermes_config` package or `hermes_store/config.py` |
| **P0-b Personas T1** | `/v1/personas` CRUD → Postgres; retire YAML write in [`routes/personas.py`](packages/nimbusware_api/routes/personas.py); materialized `PersonaCatalog` in [`hermes_extensions/personas.py`](packages/hermes_extensions/personas.py); keep `persona.shelf.updated` | API, extensions, console read path |
| **P0-c Roles T1** | Unify [`hermes_roles_registry`](packages/hermes_store/schema/postgres.sql) with full registry; materialize [`RoleRegistry`](packages/hermes_orchestrator/registry.py); drop file read when DB mode | orchestrator, app lifespan |
| **P0-d Workflows T1** | Workflow profiles in Postgres; [`integrator_workflow_apply`](packages/nimbusware_console/integrator_workflow_apply.py) / ingress read materialized profiles | API optional admin routes, orchestrator |
| **P0-e Policy snapshot** | `run.created` embeds frozen `policy_snapshot` from **materialized** merge (§6.3A), not live file reads | [`ingress.py`](packages/hermes_orchestrator/ingress.py), event payload |
| **P0-f Gitops CLI** | `hermes config import --from-repo` / `export` for bootstrap and review | `scripts/` or `preflight_cli` sibling |
| **P0-g T2 policies** | Escalation, integrator thresholds, self-refinement, critique pairings, `model-routing` policy slices → Postgres + materialize | existing `workflow_*` / loader modules |

**Tests per slice:** integration tests with Postgres; unit tests for materializer validation and
cache invalidation; no dual-write assertions.

**Stay on disk:** FAISS binaries, scraper artifact files, optional **exported** YAML (non-authoritative).

## Configuration authority (spec summary)

Aligns with [hermes-orchestrator-local-plan.md §19.5](hermes-orchestrator-local-plan.md).

| Layer | Rule |
|-------|------|
| **Source of truth** | PostgreSQL versioned rows, validated by existing Pydantic modules (`hermes_extensions.personas`, workflow parsers, escalation loaders, etc.). |
| **Materialization** | `ConfigMaterializer` (name TBD) builds refreshable in-memory catalogs at startup and on `persona.shelf.updated` / `config.document.updated` (or LISTEN/NOTIFY). |
| **Consumers** | Orchestrator, ingress, API, Streamlit—**no** direct `atomic_write_yaml` / `yaml.safe_load(configs/...)` on hot paths after migration. |
| **Run boundary** | `policy_snapshot` on `run.created` is a deep copy of materialized effective config at create time (§6.3A). |
| **Gitops** | `hermes config export` / `import` / `seed-from-repo`; exported `configs/**` is **non-authoritative** unless import is explicitly run. |
| **Forbidden** | Dual-write YAML + Postgres; per-request file reads post-migration; ad-hoc config DSL. |

**Current file-backed surfaces (retired in DB mode; file fallback when DB unset):**

- [`configs/personas/shelves.yaml`](configs/personas/shelves.yaml) ← Postgres `personas/shelves` via [`persist.py`](packages/nimbusware_config/persist.py)
- [`configs/roles.yaml`](configs/roles.yaml) ← Postgres `roles/registry` via [`ConfigMaterializer`](packages/nimbusware_config/materializer.py)
- [`configs/workflows/*.yaml`](configs/workflows/) ← Postgres `workflows/{profile}` via [`persist.py`](packages/nimbusware_config/persist.py)

---

## Strategic direction (May 2026 onward)

**Current posture:** **v1 sign-off complete** (§14 **21/21**). **v2 shipped:** operator console + micro-slice engine (fo150–fo155). **v3 shipped:** **Lane M** maker app (~98%). **v4 shipped:** **Lane U** — Maker = user console, Admin Console = admin/dev-only. **Lane R complete:** maintainability refactor (fo400–fo407 + follow-on). Default work = **regression hold** + optional polish.

**North star (Lane M):** *Local-first software creation* — Hermes enforces adversarial micro-slices; Nimbusware **Maker** gives project-scoped UX, slice approval/revert, plain-language progress, and honest hardware/model guidance (not operator telemetry).

**North star (Lane U):** *Two audiences, one platform* — users live in Maker; admins and developers use **Admin Console** for config, fleet, and diagnostics. Default installs expose Maker only; admins unlock both.

**Previous north star (v2, shipped):** *Adversarial agentic workflow orchestration* with Cursor-style **operator chat** for power users; engine enforces micro-slices instead of whole-repo rewrites.

**Hold:** fo150–fo207, Phase 3–4, §14 — regression-only unless fixing bugs.

## Product priorities (v2 — shipped)

**Status:** Epics **fo150–fo154** meet core exit criteria (May 2026). Remaining work is **polish** only unless you explicitly expand scope.

**North star:** *Adversarial agentic workflow orchestration* (Hermes) with *operator UX* (Nimbusware Streamlit) that feels like **Cursor-style chat** for configuring and launching work, while the engine enforces **micro-slices** instead of whole-repo rewrites.

### Why micro-slices (design contract)

| Goal | Mechanism |
|------|-----------|
| **Safer / fewer mistakes** | Each slice has a bounded diff budget, mandatory verify + critic + test gates before the next slice |
| **Runnable on weaker hardware** | Role agents receive **slice packets** (files, diff summary, failing test output, verdict JSON) — not full-repo context |
| **Adversarial quality** | Writer ↔ critic ↔ test roles disagree under [`unanimous_gate`](packages/hermes_orchestrator/unanimous_gate.py); slices retry or escalate instead of silently stacking debt |
| **Operator clarity** | Streamlit shows slice index, gate matrix row, and chat thread tied to the active run |

### v2 epic queue (shipped — reference)

| Order | Epic | Outcome | Primary touches |
|-------|------|---------|-----------------|
| 1 | **fo150** | **Cursor-like operator chat** — **shipped** in Streamlit: thread per session/run, message list, compose box, slash commands for “create run”, “attach persona”, “show timeline” | New `packages/nimbusware_console/operator_chat.py`, [`app.py`](packages/nimbusware_console/app.py) sidebar or dedicated page, optional `POST /v1/chat` or session-state + existing `/v1/runs` |
| 2 | **fo151** | **Custom agents** — **shipped** — create/list/select agents; each agent has **name, role binding, dedicated system prompt**; **pencil icon** opens prompt editor (save to Postgres config store T1/T2) | Config keys e.g. `agents/{id}`, Streamlit agent gallery, wire `metadata.custom_agent_id` on `run.created` |
| 3 | **fo152** | **Micro-slice orchestration model** — **shipped** — workflow + `stage_graph` extension: `slice.max_files`, `slice.max_loc`, planner emits `slice.plan` artifact; implementation stage scoped to slice id | [`stage_graph.py`](packages/hermes_orchestrator/stage_graph.py), [`pipeline.py`](packages/hermes_orchestrator/pipeline.py), `configs/workflows/micro_slice.yaml`, events `slice.planned` / `slice.completed` |
| 4 | **fo153** | **Per-slice critique + test gates** — **shipped** — after each slice verify: implementation critique → test writer (scoped tests) → unanimous gate; **no next slice** until PASS | Reuse universal critique + verify scanners; slice-scoped pytest/bandit/ruff invocations; timeline `slice_id` on gate events |
| 5 | **fo154** | **Small context handoff packets** — **shipped** — structured `SliceContextPacket` (paths, diff stat, test log excerpt, prior verdicts) passed between roles; LLM prompts reference packet only | [`agent_core`](packages/agent_core/) models, [`llm_plan.py`](packages/hermes_orchestrator/llm_plan.py) prompt assembly, max token caps per role |

**Phase 3 epics (fo143–fo146)** are **shipped** as post-verify critic **stages** on the full `lifecycle/verify` path. **Polish:** run equivalent evidence inside micro-slice `slice.critique`, or enable P3 profiles on `nimbusware_production` by default (today they are opt-in YAML profiles).

#### fo150 — Streamlit operator chat (Cursor-like for agent setup)

**Goal:** Operators configure and steer Hermes **through conversation**, not only static expanders.

**Deliverables:**

- Streamlit **chat panel**: user/assistant messages, scrollback, input at bottom; optional “thinking” / tool-call status lines when API returns run events.
- **Session model:** `st.session_state` thread id; optional persist lightweight transcript in `.cache/nimbusware_chat/` (gitignored).
- **Actions from chat:** parse intents or explicit buttons — “Start run”, “Use agent X”, “Show last gate failure”; call existing `POST /v1/runs`, `GET …/timeline`.
- **Hermes agent boundary:** chat UI is Nimbusware product layer; orchestration still flows through Nimbusware API (no second orchestrator).
- **Tests:** `tests/test_console_operator_chat.py` (render smoke, message append, run launch mock).

**Out of scope for fo150:** full IDE code editor; multi-user chat server; replacing Streamlit.

#### fo151 — Custom agents + editable prompts (pencil UI)

**Goal:** Operators define **their own agents** (not only fixed `roles.yaml` personas) with **dedicated system prompts** editable in UI.

**Deliverables:**

- **Agent registry** document in config store: `id`, `display_name`, `description`, `bound_role_id` (optional), **`system_prompt`** (markdown/text), `created_at` / `version`.
- Streamlit **agent list** + **select** drives “active agent” for chat and run defaults.
- **Pencil icon** on selected agent → `st.dialog` or expander with prompt textarea, Save/Cancel; writes via config store API (DB mode) or guarded YAML path in dev.
- **Run linkage:** `POST /v1/runs` accepts `custom_agent_id` (or persona shelf mapping); frozen on `run.created` metadata.
- **Tests:** `tests/test_custom_agents_config.py`, `tests/test_console_custom_agents.py`.

**Out of scope for fo151:** arbitrary Python tool plugins per agent; marketplace sharing.

#### fo152 — Micro-slice change model (orchestrator)

**Goal:** Hermes plans and implements **one small slice at a time** with explicit bounds.

**Deliverables:**

- Workflow profile **`micro_slice`** (or `nimbusware_production` opt-in block): `slice: { max_files: N, max_loc: M, allowed_globs: [...] }`.
- Planner stage emits **`slice.plan`** JSON: `slice_id`, `rationale`, `target_paths`, `acceptance_criteria`.
- Implementation writer receives **only** plan paths; verifier rejects diffs exceeding slice budget (deterministic check before LLM).
- Timeline summary: `current_slice`, `slices_completed`, `slices_blocked`.
- **Tests:** `tests/test_micro_slice_plan.py`, `tests/test_micro_slice_diff_budget.py`.

**Out of scope for fo152:** automatic git commit per slice (optional later); cross-repo slices.

#### fo153 — Per-slice critique + test gates

**Goal:** **Every slice** passes adversarial critique and **scoped tests** before the pipeline advances.

**Deliverables:**

- Stage graph: `slice.implement` → `slice.verify` → `slice.critique` → `slice.test` → `slice.gate` → (next slice or complete).
- Test writer runs **targeted** pytest/unittest subset from slice plan (file paths → test mapping heuristic v1).
- Reuse [`unanimous_gate.py`](packages/hermes_orchestrator/unanimous_gate.py); failing slice sets `slice.status=blocked` and surfaces in Streamlit chat + timeline.
- Integrate existing ruff/bandit/mypy verify output as **evidence** on the slice gate (feeds fo143+ later).
- **Tests:** `tests/test_micro_slice_gate_chain.py`, extend critique router tests with `slice_id` metadata.

**Out of scope for fo153:** full CI farm per slice; flaky-test quarantine product.

#### fo154 — Small context packets (role handoffs)

**Goal:** Each role receives a **bounded packet** instead of whole-repo prompts — enabling weaker GPUs and clearer adversarial separation.

**Deliverables:**

- Pydantic **`SliceContextPacket`**: `slice_id`, `paths`, `diff_unified` (capped), `test_output` (capped), `prior_verdicts[]`, `policy_excerpt`.
- Builders in orchestrator assemble packet after each gate; writers/critics consume packet in [`llm_plan.py`](packages/hermes_orchestrator/llm_plan.py) when `HERMES_USE_LLM=1`.
- Env caps: `HERMES_SLICE_PACKET_MAX_CHARS`, per-role overrides.
- Console: “View context packet” expander on active slice (read-only JSON).
- **Tests:** `tests/test_slice_context_packet.py`, packet size enforcement tests.

**v2 exit criterion:** **Met** — operator chat, custom agents, ≥2 slices with gates, capped packets (tests under `tests/test_micro_slice*.py`, `test_console_operator_chat.py`, etc.).

## Lane M — Maker product (fo300–fo308)

**Depends on:** Phase **P** shipped (micro-slice, gates, packets, `apply_slice_file_edits`); Individual local-first posture.

### Shipped (May 2026)

| Phase | Epics | Proof |
|-------|-------|-------|
| **M-A** | fo300, fo301, fo307 | `nimbusware_maker/`, `GET/POST /v1/projects`, `GET /v1/platform/readiness`, `project_id` on runs, `nimbusware-run` → Maker |

### Remaining polish (optional — does not block Lane U)

| Item | Notes |
|------|--------|
| User-scoped project create (no admin header) | **Shipped** (Lane U fo311) |
| Git worktree snapshots (vs tarball) | Documented fallback in fo305 risk notes |

### Why Lane M (product gap)

| Today (operator console) | Target (maker shell) |
|--------------------------|----------------------|
| Timeline JSON, fo133 explainers, CSV exports | Plain-language status (“Slice 2 passed — 3 files changed”) |
| Runs against Hermes repo / generic workspace | **Project** folder = the product under construction |
| Auto-advance slice chain after gates | **Approve plan** / **preview diff** / **revert slice** at boundaries |
| Preflight exists but ops-facing | **Readiness home** — Ollama, model, RAM, “use smaller model” guidance |
| LLM slice patches only | **Agent tool runtime** (read/grep/edit/shell) + snapshots + revert API |

### Epic queue (fo300–fo308)

| Order | Epic | Outcome | Primary touches |
|-------|------|---------|-----------------|
| 1 | **fo300** | **Maker app shell** | New `packages/nimbusware_maker/` or `app_maker.py`; pywebview route; Simple/Advanced toggle to operator console |
| 2 | **fo301** | **Project model** | `Project` API + store; workspace path; greenfield templates; `project_id` on `run.created` |
| 3 | **fo307** | **Local readiness** | `GET /v1/platform/readiness`; maker home strip; model presets (`fast` / `careful`) |
| 4 | **fo302** | **Intent intake** | Business prompt UI → clarifications → requirements artifact metadata |
| 5 | **fo303** | **Plain-language progress** | Maker projections; test summary card; suppress operator metrics in Simple mode |
| 6 | **fo304** | **Slice approval UX** | Plan approve gate; diff preview; apply/skip/revert; block auto slice chain until approved |
| 7 | **fo305** | **Workspace snapshots + revert** | Snapshot before slice apply; `POST …/workspace/revert`; `workspace.reverted` event |
| 8 | **fo306** | **Agent tool runtime** | `packages/hermes_agent_tools/`; allowlist; wire `slice.implement` when `HERMES_SLICE_IMPLEMENT=agent` |
| 9 | **fo308** | **First-run wizard** | Desktop install flow: folder → readiness → first maker run |

### Lane M — recommended build path

Build in **four phases** so each slice is shippable and testable. Do **not** block fo300 on fo306 — approval/revert and plain progress deliver value before full agent tools.

#### Phase M-A — Maker shell + project binding (fo300, fo301, fo307)

**Goal:** User opens maker app, picks a project folder, sees readiness, starts a `micro_slice` run scoped to that workspace.

| Deliverable | Notes |
|-------------|--------|
| Maker entrypoint | Separate Streamlit app or routed pages; hide config tooling by default |
| `Project` CRUD | Persist path, name, template, default profile (`micro_slice` + conservative budgets) |
| Run linkage | `POST /v1/runs` accepts `project_id`; orchestrator uses `project.workspace_path` not install root |
| Readiness strip | Ollama ping, model name, optional RAM hint; link to install docs when failing |
| Tests | `tests/maker/test_project_api.py`, smoke import maker app |

**Exit:** Create project → readiness green → start run → see plain “Run started” (not timeline JSON).

#### Phase M-B — Plain progress + intent (fo302, fo303)

**Goal:** Business prompt becomes a requirements artifact; progress reads in plain English.

| Deliverable | Notes |
|-------------|--------|
| Intent wizard | 3–5 clarifying questions (structured); freeze on `run.created.metadata.requirements` |
| Maker timeline projection | Map gate/slice events → sentences; slice index / total |
| Test summary card | Parse pytest output → pass/fail bullets (reuse slice verify logs) |
| Simple mode filter | Hide fo133, CSV download, operator metrics from maker views |

**Exit:** User enters intent → sees plan summary in plain language → slice status updates without opening run detail expanders.

#### Phase M-C — Approval + revert (fo304, fo305)

**Goal:** Human controls at slice boundaries; safe undo.

| Deliverable | Notes |
|-------------|--------|
| Plan approval gate | Orchestrator waits for `slice.plan.approved` event or API before first implement |
| Diff preview UI | Unified diff for pending slice; Apply / Skip buttons |
| Workspace snapshot | Before `apply_slice_file_edits`: git stash, worktree, or tarball ref stored on run |
| Revert API | `POST /v1/runs/{id}/workspace/revert` restores last approved snapshot |
| Pause auto chain | `lifecycle/slice` respects `awaiting_approval` flag |

**Exit:** User previews diff → applies → reverts one slice → workspace restored; events auditable.

#### Phase M-D — Agent substrate + polish (fo306, fo308)

**Goal:** Tool-using implementer; polished first-run experience.

| Deliverable | Notes |
|-------------|--------|
| Agent tool package | read, grep, write (plan-bound), shell (pytest/ruff allowlist) |
| `HERMES_SLICE_IMPLEMENT=agent` | Orchestrator delegates to tool loop with same gate chain |
| First-run wizard | Desktop shell: project folder, readiness, optional Ollama model pull hint |
| Continue run | Resume project’s last run with context (requirements + rejected diffs) |

**Exit:** Lane M exit criteria in local plan — ≥2 slices with agent or LLM implement, revert works, non-operator never needs config tooling.

### Lane M — dependency graph

```text
fo300 (shell) ──┬── fo301 (project) ──┬── fo302 (intent)
                │                     ├── fo303 (plain progress)
                │                     └── fo304 (approval UX)
fo307 (readiness)                     │
                                      ├── fo305 (snapshots/revert) ── fo304
                                      └── fo306 (agent tools) ── after fo305 recommended
fo308 (wizard) ── after fo300 + fo307
```

### Lane M — risk notes

| Risk | Mitigation |
|------|------------|
| Maker app duplicates operator console | Shared API/projections; maker = thin views; Advanced links to existing console |
| Snapshot storage on Windows | Prefer git worktree or stash; document disk cost for tarball fallback |
| Auto slice chain bypasses approval | Default `HERMES_SLICE_AUTO_ADVANCE=0` in maker profiles |
| Small models feel “broken” | Readiness presets + explicit “prototype mode” copy when stubs active |

## Lane U — User vs Admin consoles (fo310–fo317)

**Status:** **~100% shipped** (May 2026).  
**Depends on:** [Lane M](#lane-m--maker-product-fo300fo308) shipped (~98%).  
**Goal:** **Maker = user console**; **Admin Console** (today’s `nimbusware_console`) = **admin/dev-only** surface. Admins use **both**; default installs expose **Maker only**.

### Why Lane U (product gap)

| Today | Target |
|-------|--------|
| Both UIs are Streamlit; “operator console” competes with Maker for attention | **User console (Maker)** = product loop only; **Admin Console** = control plane |
| `nimbusware-run` defaults to Maker; `--console` still exposes full ops UI to anyone | Default desktop = Maker; Admin Console behind **admin unlock** or `nimbusware-admin` |
| `X-Nimbusware-Admin-Token` gates some routes; Maker sends it from `.env` for project create | **User routes** work without admin token; admin token unlocks admin routes + Admin Console |
| Individual edition: most `/v1` read/write is open | **UserDep** + scoped projects/runs; **AdminDep** for config, fleet, lifecycle overrides |
| Advanced Maker tab says “run operator console manually” | Admin unlock → **Open Admin Console** (gated deep link / second entrypoint) |

**Technology note:** Lane U does **not** replace Streamlit. It enforces **roles**, **API boundaries**, and **packaging** so the admin app can shrink to dev/ops without blocking the user product.

### Target roles

| Role | UI | API posture |
|------|-----|-------------|
| **User** (default) | Maker only — projects, intent, build, review, plain progress | User-scoped runs/projects; maker approval routes on own runs |
| **Admin** | Maker + Admin Console | Admin token (Individual) or admin-scoped API key (Enterprise); config, fleet, exports, lifecycle overrides |
| **Dev / power operator** (end state) | Admin Console via CLI/dev install profile | Full timeline, config tooling, OpenAPI debugging — not in default installer |

### Capability map (what lives where)

| Capability | User (Maker) | Admin Console |
|------------|--------------|---------------|
| First-run / readiness | ✓ Home + wizard | Diagnostics only |
| Project pick / create | ✓ Own projects (**add** — today POST requires admin) | All projects + delete |
| Business intent → run | ✓ | View raw metadata |
| Plain progress | ✓ | Optional deep link |
| Plan / slice approve / revert | ✓ | Audit + manual override |
| Run history (plain, per project) | ✓ **add** | Full filters + CSV export |
| Continue / resume run | ✓ **add** (fo308 partial) | ✓ |
| Model preset (fast / careful) | ✓ **add** | Full routing editor |
| Operator chat / arbitrary steering | ✗ | ✓ |
| Timeline, critic matrix, fo133 explainers | ✗ | ✓ |
| Config tooling (workflows, personas, bundles) | ✗ | ✓ |
| Custom agents CRUD | ✗ | ✓ |
| Fleet / enterprise dashboards | ✗ | ✓ |
| Lifecycle force (retry, escalate, role execute) | ✗ | ✓ |

### Epic queue (fo310–fo317)

| Order | Epic | Outcome | Primary touches |
|-------|------|---------|-----------------|
| 1 | **fo310** | **Naming + launch gates** | Rename “operator console” → **Admin Console**; `nimbusware-admin` entrypoint; Maker admin unlock UI |
| 2 | **fo311** | **User API surface** | `UserDep`; user-scoped `GET/POST /projects`; user run create/list on accessible projects |
| 3 | **fo312** | **Admin API surface** | Admin-only route group; OpenAPI tags `user` vs `admin`; 401/403 copy for Maker |
| 4 | **fo313** | **Maker user parity** | Project create without env admin token; per-project run history; Settings tab (preset, auto-advance) |
| 5 | **fo314** | **Admin Console gate** | Admin Console requires admin session at load; strip duplicated onboarding |
| 6 | **fo315** | **Packaging** | Default installer = Maker + API; admin/dev profile adds admin script; launcher “Admin” only when unlocked |
| 7 | **fo316** | **Enterprise IAM roles** | `maker_user` / `maker_admin` (or scopes); tenant project isolation |
| 8 | **fo317** | **Cross-console deep links** | Admin run detail → “Open in Maker Review”; Maker errors → admin-only diagnostics link |

### Lane U — recommended build path

Build **after Lane M exit**. Do **not** gate Admin Console on API enforcement only (U-A without U-B is cosmetic).

#### Phase U-A — Naming + launch gates (fo310)

**Goal:** Clear mental model; users do not accidentally land in admin UI.

| Deliverable | Notes |
|-------------|--------|
| Rename UI | **Admin Console** in titles, README, launcher copy |
| Desktop entrypoints | `nimbusware-run` → Maker; `nimbusware-admin` or `--admin` → Admin Console + API |
| Maker admin unlock | Sidebar “Sign in as admin” (token once per session) → **Open Admin Console** |
| Browse without admin env | Home / Build / Progress work without `NIMBUSWARE_ADMIN_TOKEN` in `.env` |

**Exit:** Fresh install user never sees Admin Console unless they opt in.

#### Phase U-B — API authorization layers (fo311, fo312)

**Goal:** Enforce user vs admin at the API.

| Deliverable | Notes |
|-------------|--------|
| `UserDep` | Individual: implicit local user; Enterprise: API key with user scope |
| Project routes | `GET /projects` user-scoped; `POST /projects` → **user** (own workspace); `DELETE` → admin |
| Run routes | User: CRUD on runs for accessible projects; admin: all runs + lifecycle mutations |
| Maker approval routes | User on own runs; admin override optional |
| Admin-only group | Personas mutate, custom agents, bundle catalog write, `execute_role`, fleet, exports |
| Problem details | Maker shows “Admin required” on 403 |

**Exit:** Full Maker loop works with **zero** admin token; admin token only for admin routes + Admin Console.

#### Phase U-C — Grow Maker (fo313)

**Goal:** Users never need Admin Console for the product loop.

| Deliverable | Notes |
|-------------|--------|
| Projects in Maker | Create/list without admin env var |
| Run history | Per-project list, plain status, jump to Review/Progress |
| Continue run | Resume last run (requirements + pending slice) |
| Settings tab | Model preset, workspace path, auto-advance (plain copy) |
| Simple mode default | No Advanced affordances until admin unlock |

**Exit:** Non-admin completes ≥2 slices with approve/revert **without** opening Admin Console.

#### Phase U-D — Admin Console as admin/dev surface (fo314, fo315)

**Goal:** Admin Console stops competing with Maker.

| Deliverable | Notes |
|-------------|--------|
| Load gate | Admin Console requires admin session |
| Strip onboarding | No getting-started duplicated from Maker wizard |
| Installer profile | Default = Maker; `dev` / `admin` profile adds admin entrypoint |
| Launcher | “Run” → Maker; “Admin” only when unlocked |

**Exit:** Admin Console not in default desktop path; documented as admin/dev tool.

#### Phase U-E — Enterprise alignment (fo316, fo317)

**Goal:** Same model in multi-tenant installs.

| Deliverable | Notes |
|-------------|--------|
| IAM roles | `maker_user`, `maker_admin` (or key scopes) |
| Maker | User API key only |
| Admin Console | Admin API key; fleet + IAM panels unchanged |
| Deep links | fo317 cross-navigation between consoles |

**Exit:** Enterprise tenant user = Maker only; ops admin = both.

### Lane U — dependency graph

```text
Lane M exit (fo300–308)
        │
        ▼
U-A (fo310) naming + launch gates
        │
        ▼
U-B (fo311–312) API auth split ─────────────┐
        │                                    │
        ▼                                    ▼
U-C (fo313) grow Maker              U-D (fo314–315) admin-only console
        │                                    │
        └──────────────┬─────────────────────┘
                       ▼
              U-E (fo316–317) Enterprise + deep links
```

**Critical path:** **U-B before U-D** — console load gates without API enforcement are insufficient.

### Lane U — immediate gaps (before U-A)

| Gap | Status |
|-----|--------|
| `POST /v1/projects` requires `AdminDep` | **Fixed** — `UserDep` on create/list/get |
| Maker `api_client.post_json` always sends admin headers | **Fixed** — user headers only; admin via `admin_post_json` |
| No session concept | **Partial** — Maker admin unlock + Admin Console load gate |
| Advanced tab points to manual `streamlit run …/console` | **Fixed** — sidebar unlock → Open Admin Console |

### Lane U — exit criteria (program complete)

- [x] Default install: Maker only; Admin Console optional/hidden  
- [x] User completes project → intent → build → review → revert **without** admin token  
- [x] Admin unlocks both UIs from Maker  
- [x] Admin Console requires admin auth at load  
- [x] OpenAPI documents user vs admin route groups  
- [x] Enterprise: user vs admin API key scopes (`maker_user` / `maker_admin`)
- [x] Enterprise: distinct user vs admin API keys  
- [x] Admin Console documented as **admin/dev**, not primary product  

### Lane U — out of scope (explicit)

| Item | Rationale |
|------|-----------|
| Rewrite Streamlit to another UI stack | Both consoles stay Streamlit; shared API/projections |
| Delete Admin Console | Remains for ops/dev; demoted, not removed |
| Move config tooling into Maker | Stays admin-only |
| Single mega Streamlit app | Keep `nimbusware_maker` and `nimbusware_console` packages separate |

### Lane U — risk notes

| Risk | Mitigation |
|------|------------|
| Breaking local dev workflows that rely on open API | Individual `UserDep` = implicit single user; document admin token for config edits |
| Enterprise keys already in production | Introduce scopes; bootstrap admin keys unchanged |
| Two Streamlit apps confuse support | Rename + docs; one “Sign in as admin” path |
| Project delete needs admin | Users archive/disable in Maker; hard delete admin-only |

## Lane R — Maintainability refactor (fo400–fo407)

**Status:** **~100% — complete** (May 2026).  
**Depends on:** [Lane U](#lane-u--user-vs-admin-consoles-fo310fo317) shipped (~100%).  
**Goal:** Raise maintainability from **~6.5/10 → ~8/10** without changing product behavior — decompose Admin Console monoliths, remove legacy shims, invert layering violations, add coverage gates.

**Maturity audit (May 2026):** Architecture **8/10**, type safety **8.5/10**, tests **7.5/10**, console maintainability **~8/10** (god-module splits, shared `operator_metrics` / `explainer_panel`, explicit `run_detail` imports, zero direct `httpx` in console).

### Epic queue (fo400–fo407)

| Order | Epic | Path | Outcome | Primary touches |
|-------|------|------|---------|-----------------|
| 1 | **fo400** | **G** — Docs & governance | `ARCHITECTURE.md`, console README, track `PLAN_GAP.md` | repo root, `packages/nimbusware_console/` |
| 2 | **fo401** | **B** — Remove legacy shims | Delete unused `packages/hermes_{api,console,config,env}/` | packages, import-graph test |
| 3 | **fo402** | **C** — Projections layer | Move `preflight_timeline_summary` → `nimbusware_projections`; orchestrator ↛ API | projections, orchestrator, API |
| 4 | **fo403** | **D** — Test hygiene | `pytest-cov` in CI; ratchet floor on core packages | `pyproject.toml`, `.github/workflows/ci.yml` |
| 5 | **fo404** | **A** — Console decomposition | Split `integrator.py`, then `bundles.py`; no module >400 lines | `nimbusware_console/pages/config_tooling/` |
| 6 | **fo405** | **E** — Shared client | `nimbusware_client` HTTP + Problem+JSON helpers for Maker + Admin | new package or `nimbusware_ui_common` |

## Lane T — Maturity 8.5 program (fo520–fo545)

**Status:** **Active** (June 2026) — primary engineering program after fo511–fo515.  
**Depends on:** [Lane S](#lane-s--stabilization--maturity-fo500fo506) + [Maturity depth fo511–fo515](#maturity-depth-fo511fo520--postlane-s) complete.  
**Goal:** Raise holistic codebase maturity from **~7.8/10 → 8.5/10** without reopening normative product scope (§14, Lane M/U shipped features).

### Target scorecard (8.5 exit)

| Dimension | Baseline (Jun 2026) | 8.5 target | Primary epics |
|-----------|---------------------|------------|---------------|
| Architecture & boundaries | 8.5 | **≥8.5** (hold) | Regression-only; no new cross-layer imports |
| CI & quality gates | 8.5 | **≥8.5** | fo520, fo537–fo539, fo544 |
| Testing depth | 7.5 | **≥8.5** | fo520–fo525, fo534, fo540 |
| Type safety | 6.5 | **≥8.0** | fo526–fo531 (API strict, orchestrator wedge) |
| Maintainability | 8.0 | **≥8.5** | fo532–fo534, services pattern fo521–fo524 |
| Security & ops | 7.5 | **≥8.0** | fo538–fo539, fo541 |
| Product completeness | 8.0 | **≥8.0** (hold) | fo538 async Ollama pull |
| Documentation | 8.0 | **≥8.5** | fo545 |

**Overall exit:** Independent reviewer (or internal checklist in fo544) rates **≥8.5** on the dimensions above; `./scripts/ci_check.ps1` green; no console module &gt;400 lines without allowlist; `nimbusware_api.*` off blanket `ignore_errors`.

### Baseline metrics (lock at T0)

|--------|------------------|-------|
| CI unit tests | **~1,808** passed (subset) | `-m "not integration and not slow and not benchmark"` |
| Coverage (library subset) | **~72%** measured / **72%** floor | `pyproject.toml` omit: Streamlit `pages/**`, Maker `ui/**`, CLI/desktop |

| UI import smoke | Admin + Maker entrypoints | `test_console_page_imports.py`, `test_maker_page_imports.py` |
| Pre-commit | ruff + format + CI-parity ruff + compileall + mypy | `.pre-commit-config.yaml` |

---

### Phase T1 — UI services plane (fo520–fo525)

**Problem:** Streamlit panels embed HTTP calls; coverage omits `pages/**` and `ui/**`; regressions (e.g. missing `import streamlit`) slip through.

**Pattern (canonical):**

```text
nimbusware_{console,maker}/services/<domain>.py   # httpx via nimbusware_client; typed dict returns
nimbusware_{console,maker}/ui/<panel>.py        # Streamlit only; calls services
tests/unit/test_<pkg>_services_<domain>.py      # mock get_json/post_json; no Streamlit
```

| Deliverable | Module(s) | Replaces HTTP in |
|-------------|-----------|------------------|
| Import smoke expansion | `tests/unit/test_console_page_imports.py`, `test_maker_page_imports.py` | — |
| Run detail/list | `nimbusware_console/services/runs.py` | `pages/run_list.py`, `run_detail/{summary,timeline_core,findings,actions}.py` |
| Config editors | `nimbusware_console/services/config_editors.py` | `workflows/{persona_editor,bundle_editor}.py` |
| Operator + agents | `services/operator_chat.py`, `services/custom_agents.py` | `operator_chat.py`, `custom_agents_ui.py` |
| Enterprise fleet | `services/enterprise.py` | `enterprise_console.py` |
| Maker core | `nimbusware_maker/services/{projects,runs,approval,progress}.py` | `ui/{home,intent,approval,progress}.py` |
| Guard: no raw client in UI | `tests/unit/test_ui_no_direct_http.py` | AST: `ui/` must not import `nimbusware_client.http` except `api_client.py` |

**fo520 — Import smoke (detailed):**

| Package | Modules to import in tests |
|---------|---------------------------|
| `nimbusware_console` | `main`, `operator_chat`, `enterprise_console_ui`, `custom_agents_ui`, `pages.run_list`, `pages.run_detail`, `pages.config_tooling`, `pages.preflight_fleet` (if exists) |
| `nimbusware_maker` | `ui`, `ui.{home,intent,approval,progress,settings,wizard,ollama_models}` |

Env stubs: `NIMBUSWARE_REPO_ROOT`, `HERMES_SKIP_PREFLIGHT=1`, `NIMBUSWARE_ADMIN_TOKEN` (console tests).

**Exit T1:** Every panel with HTTP has a matching `services/*` module + unit tests; `test_ui_no_direct_http` passes; import smoke covers all `render_*` entrypoints in `main.py` / `ui/__init__.py`.

---

### Phase T2 — Mypy ratchet (fo526–fo531)

**Problem:** `ignore_errors = true` on entire `nimbusware_api.*` and `hermes_orchestrator.*` hides real typing debt.

**Strategy:** Add **narrower** `[[tool.mypy.overrides]]` blocks with `ignore_errors = false` **after** the blanket ignore (mypy uses most specific match). Expand `test_mypy_*_surface.py` guards each tranche.

| Tranche | Epic | Modules | Est. effort |
|---------|------|---------|-------------|
| A | fo526 | `nimbusware_api.schemas.*`, `errors.py`, `admin.py`, `user.py`, `access.py`, `deps.py` | 1–2 days |
| B | fo527 | `routes/platform.py`, `projects.py`, `preflight.py`, `ollama.py`, `bundles.py` (GET), `scraper_artifacts.py` | 2–3 days |
| C | fo528 | `routes/runs/list.py`, `detail.py`, `maker_progress.py` | 2 days |
| D | fo529 | `routes/runs/create.py`, `lifecycle.py`, `maker_approval.py`, `actions.py`, `personas*.py`, `custom_agents.py` | 3–4 days |
| E | fo530 | `hermes_orchestrator.{preflight,merge,ollama_*,workflow_profiles}.py` (explicit list) | 2–3 days |
| F | fo531 | Remove `nimbusware_api.*` from blanket ignore; keep `hermes_orchestrator._pipeline.*` ignored only | 1 day |

**Do not** strict-type `_pipeline/*` mixins in Lane T (defer to post-8.5); document in `hermes_orchestrator/README.md`.

**Exit T2:** `poetry run mypy packages` green with `ignore_errors` only for: `nimbusware_console.*`, `nimbusware_maker.*`, `hermes_orchestrator._pipeline.*`, desktop `nimbusware_env` subprocess modules.

### Phase T3 — Run detail barrel (fo532–fo534)

**Problem:** `pages/run_detail/_imports.py` (~745 lines) is the last explicit re-export monolith (config tooling fixed in fo513).

**Current submodules (use for split):**

| Submodule | Role |
|-----------|------|
| `_imports_common.py` | Shared types/paths |
| `_imports_display_a.py` + `/_imports_display_a/` | Findings → escalation displays |
| `_imports_display_b.py` | Remaining display re-exports |
| `_imports_tail.py` | Tail symbols |
| `_imports.py` | **Monolithic explicit import list** ← replace |

**fo533 target file:**

```python
# pages/run_detail/_imports.py (target <25 lines)
from nimbusware_console.pages.run_detail._imports_common import *  # noqa: F403
from nimbusware_console.pages.run_detail._imports_display_a import *  # noqa: F403
from nimbusware_console.pages.run_detail._imports_display_b import *  # noqa: F403
from nimbusware_console.pages.run_detail._imports_tail import *  # noqa: F403
```

**fo532:** Run `scripts/explicit_run_detail_imports.py` (or extend) to verify no missing symbols before cutover.

**Exit T3:** `_imports.py` ≤30 lines; `test_console_module_size_allowlist_is_current` has **zero** entries (or only documented exceptions); `tests/console/test_run_detail*.py` green.

### Phase T4 — Coverage ratchet (fo535–fo537)

**Problem:** Measured **~71%** but floor **70%** — headroom exists but UI omission caps signal.

| Step | Epic | Action |
|------|------|--------|
| Stabilize | fo535 | Require **≥71.5%** on 2 consecutive `ci_check` runs on `main` before ratchet |
| Ratchet | fo536 | `--cov-fail-under=72` → later **75%** (Q+1) |
| Package floors | fo537 | `scripts/coverage_package_floors.py` — fail if `hermes_store` &lt;85%, `nimbusware_config` &lt;85%, `nimbusware_projections` &lt;85% |
| Guard | — | `test_coverage_fo514.py` + extend; never add Streamlit to global denominator until T1 exit |

**Exit T4:** CI at **72%** global floor; package floors script in `ci_check` or separate workflow; measured ≥72.5% at sign-off.

## Phase 4 — Memory and optimization (shipped)

**Normative:** [hermes-orchestrator-local-plan.md §12 Phase 4](hermes-orchestrator-local-plan.md).  
**Package:** [`packages/hermes_memory/`](packages/hermes_memory/).  
**Individual edition scope:** **repo/workspace only** (`NIMBUSWARE_REPO_ROOT`); collaboration via **shared vector store snapshots** (manifest + FAISS download).  
**Enterprise edition scope:** fleet/org-wide memory index → Lane **D** **fo202** (must not ship in Individual default install).

### Design decisions (locked May 2026)

| Topic | Decision |
|-------|----------|
| **Storage default** | Postgres metadata + **local FAISS** (bundle-catalog pattern) |
| **Pluggable backend** | Interface for local FAISS + **remote canonical store** (HTTP/file manifest); hydrate local index for offline runs; **no Qdrant in v1** |
| **Embeddings** | **`deterministic`** (CI/offline) and **`ollama`** (when `HERMES_USE_LLM=1`); record `embedding_model_id` on chunks |
| **Sync** | Manifest + blob **pull/push** so teams can share indexes without fleet DB |
| **Retrieval** | **Default-on** on `nimbusware_production` / `micro_slice`; **per-run opt-out** for retrieval and/or index contribution |
| **Safety** | Retrieval **advisory**; verifiers/gates win; capped excerpts; audit `memory.retrieval.emitted` |
| **Exit (Individual)** | Capped `memory_excerpt` on micro-slice, audited retrieval, opt-out flags — **shipped** + tested |

### Phase 4 epic queue

| Order | Epic | Track | Status |
|-------|------|-------|--------|
| 1 | **fo160** | Failure memory — schema & events | **Shipped** |
| 2 | **fo161** | Chunking & index builder | **Shipped** |
| 3 | **fo162** | Local FAISS memory index | **Shipped** |
| 4 | **fo163** | Retrieval at slice/plan | **Shipped** |
| 5 | **fo164** | Workflow + run flags + console | **Shipped** |
| 6 | **fo170** | Bundle outcome events | **Shipped** |
| 7 | **fo171** | Bundle ranking memory | **Shipped** |
| 8 | **fo172** | Console bundle success analytics | **Shipped** |
| 9 | **fo180** | Replay harness CLI | **Shipped** — `hermes-memory-replay` |
| 10 | **fo181** | Golden failure fixtures | **Shipped** — `tests/fixtures/memory/` |
| 11 | **fo190** | Per-role telemetry aggregation | **Shipped** — `hermes-role-telemetry` |
| 12 | **fo191** | Model routing suggestions | **Shipped** — `hermes-routing-suggest` (read-only) |

<details>
<summary>Historical Phase 4 PR sequence (completed May 2026) — expand for traceability</summary>

1. **fo160** — Pydantic payloads, Postgres tables, `memory.*` events.  
2. **fo161** — Indexer from `event_store` (deterministic + ollama embed).  
3. **fo162** — FAISS build/search + `scripts/build_memory_faiss_index.py`.  
4. **fo164** — Workflow `memory:` block + run flags + Streamlit toggles.  
5. **fo163** — `memory_excerpt` on `SliceContextPacket` + micro-slice wiring.  
6. **fo170–fo172** — Bundle outcome memory + console.  
7. **fo180–fo181** — Replay harness + CI fixtures.  
8. **fo190–fo191** — Role telemetry + routing suggestions CLI.

</details>

#### fo160 — Memory schema and events

**Goal:** Durable, event-aligned model for memory chunks without a second source of truth.

**Deliverables:**

- New package skeleton **`packages/hermes_memory/`** (`__init__.py`, protocol types, no retrieval yet).
- Pydantic models: `MemoryChunk`, `MemoryRetrievalHit`, `MemoryIndexManifest` (chunk schema version, `embedding_mode`, `repo_root_hash`, generation id).
- Postgres tables (names TBD, e.g. `memory_chunk`, `memory_index_generation`) keyed by **repo scope** + `store_seq` / `run_id` / `finding_id` pointers.
- Optional append-only events: `memory.indexed`, `memory.retrieval.emitted` — extend `event_store` CHECK allowlist in same release as `EventType` union.
- Rebuild job: scan `event_store` for contributory runs (respect `memory.index_contribution` on `run.created`).
- **Tests:** `tests/test_hermes_memory_schema.py`, migration smoke against Postgres fixture.

**Out of scope:** FAISS files; prompt injection; remote sync.

---

#### fo161 — Chunking and index builder

**Goal:** Extract searchable chunks from failed runs and deterministic fixes.

**Deliverables:**

- Chunk sources: `finding.created` (category, severity, `required_fixes`, repro snippet caps), last `gate.decision.emitted` FAIL per stage, optional critic FAIL evidence refs.
- Redaction: repo-relative paths; max bytes per chunk; skip runs with `memory.index_contribution: false`.
- **Embedding:** `deterministic` (hash vector, align with bundle catalog); **`ollama`** path when workflow + `HERMES_USE_LLM=1`.
- Persist chunk rows + embedding metadata to Postgres (fo160 tables).
- CLI: `poetry run hermes-memory-index rebuild --repo-root .` (name TBD).
- **Tests:** fixture events → expected chunk count and stable embed hash.

**Out of scope:** FAISS write (fo162); cross-repo scope.

---

#### fo162 — Local FAISS memory index

**Goal:** Fast top-k retrieval under `configs/memory/index/` (or `.hermes/memory/index/`).

**Deliverables:**

- `hermes_memory.faiss_index`: build from Postgres chunk table; write `faiss.index` + `memory_order.json` + `manifest.json`.
- `search_memory(repo_root, query, *, k)` — parallel API to `search_bundles`.
- Stale detection: catalog mtime pattern from [`bundle_catalog.py`](packages/nimbusware_console/bundle_catalog.py).
- Env: `HERMES_MEMORY_INDEX_DIR` (override path).
- Optional poetry group reuse **`--with faiss`**.
- **Tests:** build + search round-trip; stale flag when manifest older than DB generation.

**Out of scope:** Remote push (manifest-only stub OK).

---

#### fo163 — Retrieval at slice and plan stages

**Goal:** Inject capped **memory excerpt** into micro-slice and planner context (default-on when workflow allows).

**Deliverables:**

- Extend [`SliceContextPacket`](packages/agent_core/models/slice_packet.py) with optional `memory_excerpt: str` (or parallel field in builder only).
- [`build_slice_context_packet`](packages/hermes_orchestrator/slice_context_packet.py): call `hermes_memory.retrieve()` with query = slice paths + plan rationale + last test output hash.
- Wire [`micro_slice_executor.py`](packages/hermes_orchestrator/micro_slice_executor.py) and [`llm_slice.py`](packages/hermes_orchestrator/llm_slice.py) when `memory.retrieval_enabled` on run metadata.
- Emit `memory.retrieval.emitted` with hit ids, char count, stage name.
- Env: `HERMES_MEMORY_RETRIEVAL_K`, `HERMES_MEMORY_EXCERPT_MAX_CHARS`.
- **Tests:** indexed fixture run + new run receives excerpt; opt-out run receives none.

**Out of scope:** Auto-apply patches from memory.

---

#### fo164 — Workflow block and per-run operator controls

**Goal:** Frozen memory policy on `run.created`; console/API opt-out (“do not pollute memory”).

**Deliverables:**

- Workflow YAML `memory:` block (see normative plan); parser in `hermes_orchestrator/workflow_memory.py`.
- Freeze on `run.created`: `memory_index_version`, `memory.retrieval_enabled`, `memory.index_contribution`, `embedding_mode`.
- `POST /v1/runs` body fields + Streamlit checkboxes on run create/detail.
- Timeline summary: `memory_retrieval` last event snippet.
- Default **on** for `nimbusware_production` and `micro_slice` profiles.
- **Tests:** `tests/test_workflow_memory.py`, `tests/test_console_memory_flags.py`, API create_run metadata.

**Out of scope:** Bundle memory flags (fo170).

---

#### fo170 — Bundle outcome events

**Goal:** Record integrator gate results for later ranking.

**Deliverables:**

- On integrator gate pass/fail, append metadata or lightweight event with `bundle_id`, score, `workflow_profile`, project tags.
- **Tests:** pipeline integrator hook emits structured outcome.

**Out of scope:** Changing integrator threshold logic.

---

#### fo171 — Bundle ranking memory

**Goal:** Bias `search_bundles` and integrator candidate ranking using historical success rates.

**Deliverables:**

- Aggregate table or materialized view: `bundle_id` × tag profile → success rate, sample count.
- Blend into [`search_bundles`](packages/hermes_extensions/catalog.py) ordering (configurable weight).
- **Tests:** synthetic outcomes change rank order.

---

#### fo172 — Console bundle success analytics

**Goal:** Operator read-only view of bundle memory.

**Deliverables:**

- Streamlit expander under bundle catalog: success table, sample counts, last updated.
- **Tests:** `tests/test_console_bundle_memory.py`.

---

#### fo180 — Replay harness

**Goal:** Deterministic replay of `event_store` rows into read models for regression.

**Deliverables:**

- CLI: `hermes-memory-replay` or `scripts/replay_run.py` — input `run_id`, output timeline JSON + diff mode.
- **Tests:** golden run id → stable summary hash.

---

#### fo181 — Failure pattern fixtures

**Goal:** CI guards for memory + replay stability.

**Deliverables:**

- Curated anonymized event slices under `tests/fixtures/memory/`.
- CI job step: rebuild index + assert retrieval hits stable ids.

---

#### fo190 — Per-role telemetry aggregation — **shipped**

**Goal:** Aggregate token/latency hints from event metadata per role.

**Deliverables (done):**

- [`role_telemetry.py`](packages/hermes_orchestrator/role_telemetry.py) — batch reader over recent runs; per-role stage duration, token hints, preflight rollup.
- CLI: `hermes-role-telemetry`; optional `--persist` → `policy/role-telemetry-aggregate`.
- **Tests:** [`tests/test_role_telemetry.py`](tests/test_role_telemetry.py).

---

#### fo191 — Model routing suggestions — **shipped**

**Goal:** Propose `model-routing.yaml` tweaks from fo190 aggregates (operator approve via `nimbusware-config`).

**Deliverables (done):**

- [`routing_suggestions.py`](packages/hermes_orchestrator/routing_suggestions.py) — read-only suggestions from aggregates + current routing YAML.
- CLI: `hermes-routing-suggest` — never auto-writes; apply via `nimbusware-config import`.
- **Tests:** [`tests/test_role_telemetry.py`](tests/test_role_telemetry.py) (suggestion cases).

---

**Phase 4 exit criterion (sprint board):** **Met (Individual edition, May 2026)** — micro-slice runs receive capped `memory_excerpt` when indexed failures exist; `memory.retrieval.emitted` is audited; opt-out runs skip read/write per flags. Proof: [`tests/test_hermes_memory_pipeline.py`](tests/test_hermes_memory_pipeline.py), [`tests/test_workflow_memory.py`](tests/test_workflow_memory.py).

---

## Lane D — Enterprise edition

**Goal:** A separately bootstrapped **Enterprise** edition without breaking the **Individual** (local-first) install path. Enterprise capabilities are **gated at setup** (`NIMBUSWARE_EDITION=enterprise`) so a solo operator never pulls IAM, tenancy, or fleet dependencies by default.

**Status (May 2026):** Core epics **fo200–fo207 shipped**. Lane D **exit criterion met** (two tenants, IAM-enforced API, fleet memory — see tests below). Remaining items are **ops polish**, not missing features.

### Edition split (locked May 2026)

| | **Individual** (default) | **Enterprise** (Lane D) |
|---|--------------------------|-------------------------|
| **Install** | `python scripts/install_nimbusware.py` | Same script with `--edition enterprise` (or `NIMBUSWARE_EDITION=enterprise`) |
| **Postgres** | Single local DB | Same or managed; optional read replicas later |
| **Memory index** | **Repo-scoped** only (Phase 4 shipped) | **Org/fleet-scoped** index + cross-repo retrieval (**fo202**) |
| **IAM / tenancy** | None (single operator) | RBAC, API keys, `tenant_id` on runs (**fo201**) |
| **Config freshness** | Poll / restart OK | `LISTEN/NOTIFY` + `config.document.updated` (**fo203**) |
| **Artifacts** | Local disk + optional object-store mirror | Object-store **primary** (**fo204**) |
| **Workers** | In-process + optional Redis boundary (shipped) | Multi-node Redis production profile (**fo205**) |
| **Observability** | Per-run preflight + fo190 telemetry | Fleet sustained p95 SLI + benchmark harness (**fo206**) |
| **Console** | Single workspace | Tenant switcher + fleet dashboards (**fo207**) |

**Rule:** No Enterprise-only route, table, or background job registers unless `NIMBUSWARE_EDITION=enterprise` (via **fo200** gates). Individual installs must pass the full **2397** test suite without enterprise-only runtime deps.

### Lane D epic queue

| Order | Epic | Focus | Status |
|-------|------|-------|--------|
| 1 | **fo200** | Edition bootstrap — `NIMBUSWARE_EDITION`, install profiles, compose splits, feature registry | **Shipped** |
| 2 | **fo201** | Enterprise IAM — tenants, API keys, `tenant_id` + RLS on store/memory | **Shipped** |
| 3 | **fo202** | Fleet memory — `org_scope_hash`, remote store, `hermes-memory-sync` | **Shipped** |
| 4 | **fo203** | Config NOTIFY — `config.document.updated`, materializer invalidation | **Shipped** |
| 5 | **fo204** | Object-store primary — scraper artifacts S3/file primary | **Shipped** |
| 6 | **fo205** | Redis fleet worker — compose profile, health, back-pressure | **Shipped** |
| 7 | **fo206** | Fleet Ollama SLI — sustained p95 export, pytest-benchmark harness | **Shipped** |
| 8 | **fo207** | Enterprise console — tenant switcher, fleet dashboards | **Shipped** |

### Lane D — ops polish (non-blocking)

| Item | ~% | Notes |
|------|-----|--------|
| OIDC / SSO for Streamlit | 0% | API-key auth + tenant switcher shipped; IdP integration deferred |
| K8s / Helm production charts | ~30% | `docker-compose` + runbooks; no first-class Helm chart |
| External SLI scheduling | ~50% | `hermes-fleet-ollama-sli` CLI + API; wire to cron/Prometheus is operator-owned |
| Multi-region Redis | 0% | Single Redis URL model sufficient for v1 Enterprise |

#### fo200 — Edition bootstrap (prerequisite) — **shipped**

**Goal:** One codebase, two products — selected at **install**, not compile time.

**Deliverables (done):**

- Env: `NIMBUSWARE_EDITION=individual|enterprise` (default **`individual`**) — [`edition.py`](packages/nimbusware_env/edition.py).
- [`scripts/install_nimbusware.py`](scripts/install_nimbusware.py): `--edition` flag; persists to `.env`; enterprise auto `--with-redis`.
- API: `GET /v1/platform/edition` (all editions); `/v1/enterprise/*` returns **404** on Individual.
- Runtime: `enterprise_feature_enabled()` / `require_enterprise_feature()` for fo201+ gates.
- **Tests:** [`tests/test_edition.py`](tests/test_edition.py).

**Out of scope:** fo201+ behavior (IAM, fleet memory, …).

Emits ``"Missing linter: Ruff."`` / ``"Missing linter: Bandit."`` when exactly one linter is missing, ``"Missing linters: Ruff, Bandit."`` when both are missing, and ``None`` when ``summary`` is not a mapping or when **both** linters are observable (any pass/fail combo). - **§14 #17 self-refinement description-length caption (shipped):** ``self_refinement_description_length_caption`` in ``packages/nimbusware_console/self_refinement_display.py`` reads ``description_char_len`` from :func:`self_refinement_timeline_operator_metrics` and returns ``"Description length: <N> chars."`` when the value is a positive ``int`` (``bool`` excluded). Returns ``None`` for non-mapping ``sr``, missing / non-positive / non-integer ``description_char_len``, or zero length (missing / empty description). Rendered as ``st.caption`` immediately after ``self_refinement_marker_window_caption`` inside the **Self-refinement (from timeline)** expander in ``app.py``; new unit cases (non-mapping -> None, missing description -> None, empty description -> None, 1-char -> ``Description length: 1 chars.``, 42-char -> exact count, bool / negative / non-int ``description_char_len`` guards via monkeypatch) in ``tests/test_console_self_refinement.py``.

Same swallow pattern as :func:`bundle_catalog_bundles_without_tags_count` (missing / malformed / non-dict root / non-list ``bundles`` -> ``0``). ``Bundles without id: K of M.`` ``st.caption`` in ``app.py`` when ``K > 0``, immediately below the existing without-tags caption; new unit cases (real-repo ``0 <= K <= bundle_count``, missing / malformed / non-dict / non-list ``bundles`` -> ``0``, mixed fixture with one good + three bad ids -> ``3``, all-good ids -> ``0``, unique-id fixture ``without_id + len(bundle_ids_sample(max_n=99)) == bundle_count``) in ``tests/test_console_bundle_catalog.py``.

- **#1 Ollama + model preflight — advanced sampling**: **`poetry run hermes-preflight` shipped (fo123)**; **payload extension + API timeline summary + Streamlit expander shipped (fo124)**. CLI lives in [`packages/hermes_orchestrator/preflight_cli.py`](d:\Hermes\packages\hermes_orchestrator\preflight_cli.py); supports `--config`, `--samples` (1..20), `--timeout`, `--json-probe`, `--output`; emits a single-line JSON record with `schema_version=1`, latency histogram (fixed bucket edges 50/100/250/500/1000/2500/5000/10000 ms + overflow), `samples_requested` vs `samples_used`, full evidence dict + `result.status`/`exit_code`. Mutates `HERMES_PREFLIGHT_LATENCY_SAMPLES` / `HERMES_PREFLIGHT_JSON_PROBE` only for the probe lifetime (restored on exit ⇒ reentrant). Histogram math lifted to shared module [`packages/hermes_orchestrator/preflight_histogram.py`](d:\Hermes\packages\hermes_orchestrator\preflight_histogram.py) so both CLI and Streamlit console render identical buckets. `ModelPreflightPassedPayload` now persists `health_latency_samples_ms: list[int] | None` (max 20, non-negative) — additive JSONB-safe change, legacy events default to `None`. `GET /v1/runs/{id}/timeline` exposes a new top-level `preflight` summary alongside `integrator_gate` / `agent_evaluator` / etc. (see [`preflight_timeline_summary`](d:\Hermes\packages\hermes_api\routes\runs.py)). Tests: [`tests/test_preflight_cli.py`](d:\Hermes\tests\test_preflight_cli.py) (20), [`tests/test_preflight_histogram_shared.py`](d:\Hermes\tests\test_preflight_histogram_shared.py) (6), [`tests/test_preflight_timeline_summary.py`](d:\Hermes\tests\test_preflight_timeline_summary.py) (6), [`tests/test_preflight_history_display.py`](d:\Hermes\tests\test_preflight_history_display.py) (12), [`tests/test_preflight_payload_samples_roundtrip.py`](d:\Hermes\tests\test_preflight_payload_samples_roundtrip.py) (6), plus `test_timeline_preflight_summary_from_passed_event` in [`tests/test_api.py`](d:\Hermes\tests\test_api.py). **Note (fo130):** cross-run preflight **trends** ship in the console via bounded client-side **GET …/timeline** fan-out from the last list page (see #11 / [`preflight_cross_run_display.py`](d:\Hermes\packages\hermes_console\preflight_cross_run_display.py)). **Still deferred:** a dedicated **`/v1/preflight-history`** aggregation API or multi-page / filtered fleet-wide rollups.

Optional **``POST /v1/personas/{shelf}``** for brand-new ids from the evaluator remains a later slice. Legacy fo127 spec bullets follow:
  - **Schema extension** on [`configs/personas/shelves.yaml`](d:\Hermes\configs\personas\shelves.yaml) entries: add optional `instructions` (free-form system-prompt text), `capability_profile` (string), `boundary_statement` (string), `allowed_tools` (list[str]), `success_metrics` (list[str]), `probation_status` (`"probation"` | `"promoted"` | `"shelved"`), and `version` (int, monotonic per persona id). Extend [`PersonaShelf.validate_structure`](d:\Hermes\packages\hermes_extensions\personas.py) accordingly, keeping every new field optional so legacy entries (`{id, display_name}` only) still load. Mirror the changes into [`PersonaShelf.to_public_catalog`](d:\Hermes\packages\hermes_extensions\personas.py) and the `PERSONAS_RESPONSE_200` example in [`packages/nimbusware_api/schemas/openapi.py`](d:\Hermes\packages\hermes_api\schemas\openapi.py).
  - **Write API** in [`packages/nimbusware_api/routes/personas.py`](d:\Hermes\packages\hermes_api\routes\personas.py): add `PUT /v1/personas/{shelf}/{persona_id}` (full upsert), `PATCH /v1/personas/{shelf}/{persona_id}` (partial — typically just `instructions`), `POST /v1/personas/{shelf}` (create new), and `DELETE /v1/personas/{shelf}/{persona_id}`. Each route must validate the body against the extended schema, atomically rewrite `shelves.yaml` (tmp + `os.replace` like fo126 / fo125), bump `version` on the affected entry, emit an event-store record (new `persona.shelf.updated` event type with `{shelf, persona_id, prev_version, next_version, fields_changed}`) so the audit trail lives next to runs, and return the new full catalog. All four routes must honour `Idempotency-Key` (matches the lifecycle / actions convention already in [`packages/nimbusware_api/routes/runs.py`](d:\Hermes\packages\hermes_api\routes\runs.py)).
  - **Streamlit editor** in [`packages/nimbusware_console/app.py`](d:\Hermes\packages\hermes_console\app.py) (extend the existing "Persona shelves (local repo)" expander, or add a sibling "Persona editor (writes via API)" expander): per-persona row → expand → `st.text_area("instructions")` + simple inputs for the new fields, "Save" button that hits the `PATCH` route, an `st.diff`-style preview of the change, and a freshness caption matching the fo126 pattern. Includes a "New persona" form gated on the user supplying a non-empty `id` + `shelf`. All session state must be in keys prefixed `hermes_persona_edit_*` for easy reset.
  - **Validation + safety**: server-side length caps (e.g. `instructions ≤ 8000 chars`, `capability_profile ≤ 2000`, `allowed_tools ≤ 50` entries), unicode normalisation, refusal of empty `id` / unknown shelf, refusal of `version` skew (caller must include the version they last read; mismatch ⇒ HTTP 409). The atomic rewrite uses the existing `load_yaml` reader + a sibling `dump_yaml` writer (introduce one if missing in [`packages/hermes_orchestrator/merge.py`](d:\Hermes\packages\hermes_orchestrator\merge.py)).
  - **Tests** (pivot guardrail): `tests/test_persona_shelf_schema_extension.py` (schema acceptance/rejection + legacy compat), `tests/test_personas_write_api.py` (PUT/PATCH/POST/DELETE happy + 409 version-skew + 422 length-cap), `tests/test_persona_shelf_atomic_rewrite.py` (tmp + replace, concurrent writer guard), `tests/test_console_persona_editor.py` (Streamlit form roundtrip via mocked `httpx`), plus one integration test that exercises the full edit→re-read round trip and verifies the event-store record landed.
  - **Still deferred beyond auto-promote + auto-create:** richer evaluator **LLM output** driving dynamic create/promote decisions (today’s knobs are workflow-declarative).

**Per-epic guardrails (carried forward from the fo103–fo122 era):**

1. **One epic per planning cycle.** Do NOT start the next epic until the current one is merge-ready. Parallel half-finished epics hide real delivery risk.
2. **Record the chosen epic** in the PR description AND a one-line note in this file when the epic ships.
3. **Tests still required**: every feature ships with `unit` (`tests/test_*.py`, fast) + `integration` (`tests -m integration`) coverage where applicable. The pivot is away from STANDALONE test-slice composites, not away from tests-with-features.
4. **Ruff + mypy must stay clean** at every commit (`poetry run ruff check packages tests`, `poetry run mypy packages`).
5. **Streamlit / API changes** should land OpenAPI examples + console raw-JSON expanders alongside the feature, matching the patterns already documented in §14 #3 / #11.

The legacy "Suggested next backlog" section below remains the canonical issue queue. The `fo103`–`fo122` numbered plans under `.cursor/plans/` are archived; new work is tracked per-epic.

all cases use quoted YAML scalars to bypass PyYAML's YAML 1.1 bool resolver (which would eagerly convert unquoted `TRUE` / `YES` / `On` / `False` / `no` to Python `bool` and skip the string ladder); per-iteration `case_id` message identifies any failing scalar; 2. Pick **one** item from [Active backlog](#active-backlog-may-2026), [Lane M](#lane-m--maker-product-fo300fo308), or [Lane U](#lane-u--user-vs-admin-consoles-fo310fo317)—not §14 rows or shipped fo150–fo155 / fo143–fo146 / PZ-2–PZ-10 unless fixing a bug.
3. Split into reviewable PRs; avoid parallel half-finished epics.
4. Update **Current cycle epic** at [Strategic direction](#strategic-direction-may-2026-onward) and append a **(shipped)** bullet under the epic before starting the next.

## Poetry optional groups and FAISS

- Default install: `poetry install` — main deps + **`[tool.poetry.group.dev]`** (pytest, ruff, mypy, etc.).
- Optional FAISS: **`poetry install --with faiss`** installs **`[tool.poetry.group.faiss]`** (`faiss-cpu`), used by bundle index tooling (e.g. `scripts/build_bundle_faiss_index.py`).
- **Rebuild triggers:** run the script after **`configs/bundles/catalog.yaml`** (or bundle list semantics) change, or when the console/API reports **`stale`** (catalog newer on disk than ``faiss.index`` / ``bundle_order.json``). Defaults write under **`configs/bundles/index/`** (same as **`GET /v1/bundles/search`** vector path).
- CI: **`ci.yml`** unit job uses **`poetry install`** only (no FAISS on every push/PR). Optional index smoke: **`.github/workflows/bundle_faiss_index.yml`** runs **`poetry install --with faiss`** + **`scripts/build_bundle_faiss_index.py`** on a **weekly** schedule and on **`workflow_dispatch`**; **`--help`** lists ``--repo-root`` / ``--catalog`` / ``--out-dir``.

## Preflight sustained sampling (tradeoffs)

- **`HERMES_PREFLIGHT_LATENCY_SAMPLES`** drives bounded multisample timing on the health probe during `run.start` (hard cap 20); raising N improves local p95 stability but slows every cold start.
- **Sustained** production p95 (SLI-style over hours) is not implemented in-repo; use external metrics or an offline probe if you need fleet-wide latency SLOs.
- **Operator playbook (local API scope):** keep **`HERMES_SKIP_PREFLIGHT=1`** in CI and focused tests; for realistic cold starts leave preflight on and accept higher **`run.start`** latency when **`HERMES_PREFLIGHT_LATENCY_SAMPLES`** is raised above **1**. Treat persisted multisample metadata on **`model.preflight.passed`** as **debugging signal**, not an SLI—Prometheus/Grafana or host metrics remain the right place for hours-long p95. **`HERMES_PREFLIGHT_JSON_PROBE`** toggles JSON-shape checks on the probe when you need stricter Ollama contract validation.

## Verification

**Environment:** copy **[`.env.example`](.env.example)** to **`.env`** at the repo root (gitignored). Hermes loads it via **`nimbusware_env.load_dotenv()`** in API, console, CLIs, pytest, and install scripts.

**First-time setup:** from the repo root, run **`.\scripts\install-nimbusware.ps1`** (Windows) or **`bash scripts/install-nimbusware.sh`** (Unix). That checks Python/Poetry, runs **`poetry install`**, and if PostgreSQL is not running shows an **interactive menu** (Docker Compose, Windows `.exe` download, winget, manual, custom URL, or skip) with short explanations per option. Non-interactive: **`--non-interactive`** or **`--postgres-choice docker|native|skip|...`**. Applies **`postgres.sql`** when a DB is available. See **`python scripts/install_nimbusware.py --help`**.

```powershell
Set-Location d:\Hermes
poetry run pytest tests -q -m "not integration"
poetry run pytest tests -m integration
poetry run pytest tests/test_extensions_yaml.py -q
poetry run ruff check packages tests
poetry run mypy packages
```

The last line is a quick guard for the `hermes_extensions` ↔ `hermes_orchestrator` import cycle (lazy `RunOrchestrator` on the orchestrator package).

### Integration parity (matches `.github/workflows/ci.yml` `integration` job)

1. Run Postgres locally and set **`NIMBUSWARE_DATABASE_URL`** (same URL style as CI: `postgresql://user:pass@host:5432/dbname`).
2. Apply [`packages/hermes_store/schema/postgres.sql`](d:\Hermes\packages\hermes_store\schema\postgres.sql) (via `scripts/apply_event_store.sh`) then integration tests in one step:
   - **Windows (PowerShell):**  
     `$env:NIMBUSWARE_DATABASE_URL = "postgresql://nimbusware:nimbusware@127.0.0.1:5432/hermes"`  
     `.\scripts\run_integration_like_ci.ps1`
   - **Unix:**  
     `export NIMBUSWARE_DATABASE_URL=postgresql://nimbusware:nimbusware@127.0.0.1:5432/hermes`  
     `bash scripts/run_integration_like_ci.sh`
3. Alternatively apply only: **`.\scripts\apply_event_store.ps1`** or **`bash scripts/apply_event_store.sh`**, then run **`poetry run pytest tests -q -m integration`** with **`HERMES_SKIP_PREFLIGHT=1`** and **`NIMBUSWARE_REPO_ROOT`** set to the repo root.

**Env:** `HERMES_SKIP_PREFLIGHT`, `HERMES_USE_LLM`, `HERMES_RUN_BANDIT`, `HERMES_PREFLIGHT_JSON_PROBE`, **`HERMES_PREFLIGHT_LATENCY_SAMPLES`**, **`HERMES_EMIT_INTEGRATOR_GATE`** (`0`/`false`/`no` forces integrator gate emission off; `1`/`true`/`yes` forces on; when unset, emission follows **`configs/integrator/thresholds.yaml`** **`enabled`** or workflow **`integrator_gate.enabled`** in **`configs/workflows/{profile}.yaml`**), **`HERMES_INTEGRATOR_MIN_SCORE_TO_PASS`** (non-empty float `0..1` overrides workflow **`integrator_gate.min_score_to_pass`** and **`configs/integrator/thresholds.yaml`** **`min_score_to_pass`** for the bundle compatibility gate; invalid value ignored so YAML applies), **`HERMES_ALLOW_WORKFLOW_YAML_WRITE`** (truthy `1`/`true`/`yes`/`on` allows Streamlit **Apply integrator_gate to disk** to merge + rewrite **only** the **`integrator_gate`** subtree in **`configs/workflows/{profile}.yaml`** via **`atomic_write_yaml`**; otherwise writes are blocked), **`HERMES_OUTBOUND_FETCH_ENABLED`** (truthy allows outbound GET for **`egress_checked_fetch_url`** and **`scraper:fetch`**), **`HERMES_AGENT_EVALUATOR`** (`0`/`false`/`no` forces agent-evaluator **`stage.started`** off including workflow-opt-in; `1`/`true`/`yes` forces on; when unset, emission follows workflow **`agent_evaluator.enabled`** in **`configs/workflows/{profile}.yaml`**), **`HERMES_ATTACH_SECURITY_SCAN_METADATA`** (`0`/`false`/`no` suppresses **`security_scan_*`** on verifier **`finding.created`** even when workflow **`security_scan_metadata_on_verify`** is true; `1`/`true`/`yes` forces attachment; when unset, follow workflow YAML in **`configs/workflows/{profile}.yaml`**), **`HERMES_IMPLEMENTATION_CRITIQUE_LLM`** (truthy: after **implementation** verifier, try Ollama JSON **`implementation.critique`** via [`execute_implementation_critique_llm`](d:\Hermes\packages\hermes_orchestrator\llm_plan.py) when a **preflight-selected** model exists; default off), **`HERMES_STUB_IMPLEMENTATION_CRITICS`** (truthy: append stub **`implementation.critique`** when LLM path did not emit events; can combine with LLM env as fallback), **`HERMES_IMPLEMENTATION_CRITIQUE_STAGE_FAILED_ON_GATE_FAIL`** (truthy: after verify, emit **`stage.failed`** when the last **`implementation.critique`** **`gate.decision.emitted`** is FAIL; default off), **`HERMES_ENABLE_TEST_WRITER_CRITIQUE`** (master switch for optional **`test_writer.critique`** after implementation critique; default off), **`HERMES_TEST_WRITER_CRITIQUE_LLM`** (truthy: try Ollama JSON **`test_writer.critique`** when master switch on and a preflight-selected model exists), **`HERMES_STUB_TEST_WRITER_CRITICS`** (truthy: stub **`test_writer.critique`** when master switch on and LLM path did not emit events), **`HERMES_TEST_WRITER_CRITIQUE_STAGE_FAILED_ON_GATE_FAIL`** (truthy: after optional test-writer critique, emit **`stage.failed`** when the last **`test_writer.critique`** **`gate.decision.emitted`** is FAIL; default off), **`HERMES_ENABLE_PLANNER_CRITIQUE`** (master switch for optional **`planner.critique`** after test-writer critique; default off), **`HERMES_PLANNER_CRITIQUE_LLM`** (truthy: try Ollama JSON **`planner.critique`** when master switch on and a preflight-selected model exists), **`HERMES_STUB_PLANNER_CRITICS`** (truthy: stub **`planner.critique`** when master switch on and LLM path did not emit events), **`HERMES_PLANNER_CRITIQUE_STAGE_FAILED_ON_GATE_FAIL`** (truthy: after optional planner critique, emit **`stage.failed`** when the last **`planner.critique`** **`gate.decision.emitted`** is FAIL; default off), **`HERMES_IMPLEMENTATION_CRITIQUE_HARD_BLOCK_ON_GATE_FAIL`**, **`HERMES_TEST_WRITER_CRITIQUE_HARD_BLOCK_ON_GATE_FAIL`**, **`HERMES_PLANNER_CRITIQUE_HARD_BLOCK_ON_GATE_FAIL`** (truthy: skip integrator / agent-evaluator / self-refinement tail when that stage's last critique gate is FAIL; non-truthy env value disables hard-block for that stage when env is non-empty); critique envs **override** frozen workflow **`universal_critique`** for the same knob when the env value is **non-empty** (empty → YAML). **`HERMES_SCRAPER_ARTIFACT_DIR`** (optional override for scraper response artifact base directory; unset → **`<repo>/.cache/hermes_scraper`**), **`HERMES_SCRAPER_ARTIFACT_MAX_AGE_DAYS`** (optional positive integer for [`scripts/prune_scraper_artifacts.py`](d:\Hermes\scripts\prune_scraper_artifacts.py); omit **`--max-age-days`** to use this env), `NIMBUSWARE_ADMIN_TOKEN`, `NIMBUSWARE_DATABASE_URL`, **`NIMBUSWARE_ROLES_FROM_DB`** (truthy with DB URL → load role registry from Postgres), `NIMBUSWARE_REPO_ROOT`.

## End-to-end operator validation

**Status:** **Harness shipped** (rounds 343–349) — `scripts/install_nimbusware.py`, `scripts/ollama_setup.py`, and `scripts/e2e_smoke.py` green on configured hosts (`--profile app` without Postgres; `--profile full` with schema + integration + unit aggregate).  
**Remaining:** optional **CI workflow** (matrix install + smoke); document Windows-native golden path in runbooks; do not block B1 on E2E CI unless releasing install UX.

**Goal:** On a clean machine, prove **install → Postgres → schema → API → console → one run** without manual guesswork and matches CI expectations.

### Scope

| Layer | What “green” means | How to verify (initial) |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Bootstrap** | `install_nimbusware.py` finishes; Poetry env usable | `python scripts/install_nimbusware.py --postgres-choice docker` (CI-like) or native/manual on Windows |
| **PostgreSQL** | `NIMBUSWARE_DATABASE_URL` accepts connections; `hermes` DB exists | `poetry run python -c "import psycopg; psycopg.connect(...)"` or `psql` |
| **Schema** | `postgres.sql` applied; event store tables present | `scripts/apply_event_store.ps1` / `.sh`; spot-check `\dt` or integration fixture |
| **Config seed** | Optional `nimbusware-config seed-from-repo` when using DB config | `poetry run nimbusware-config seed-from-repo` |
| **Unit gate** | Fast tests pass without Postgres | `poetry run pytest tests -q -m "not integration"` |
| **Integration gate** | Postgres-backed tests pass | `scripts/run_integration_like_ci.ps1` |
| **API** | `nimbusware-api` serves `/v1` health or OpenAPI | Start `poetry run nimbusware-api`; `GET /docs` or `GET /v1/runs` |
| **Console** | Streamlit app loads against API | `poetry run streamlit run packages/nimbusware_console/app.py` (smoke: no import error) |
| **Run smoke** | `POST /v1/runs` returns 201; timeline has expected events | One pytest module or `scripts/e2e_smoke.py` (to add) with `HERMES_SKIP_PREFLIGHT=1` |
| **LLM (optional)** | Ollama preflight passes when enabled | `poetry run hermes-preflight` with Ollama running; separate from default E2E |

### Deliverables (implementation checklist)

1. **`scripts/e2e_smoke.py`** — **shipped** — orchestrates the table above; exits non-zero on first failure; supports `--skip-integration`, `--skip-install-check`, `--no-docker`. Run: `poetry run python scripts/e2e_smoke.py`. Pytest wrapper: [`tests/e2e/test_operator_smoke.py`](tests/e2e/test_operator_smoke.py).
2. **CI job** — optional `workflow_dispatch` workflow (or nightly) that runs install + integration + smoke on `ubuntu-latest` + Windows runner matrix (Windows only for native-install path).
3. **Documented golden path** in this section — copy-paste commands for Docker vs Windows native vs skip-Postgres dev.
4. **Promotion rule** — E2E smoke must pass locally before marking §14 B1 rows **Done** when they depend on Postgres or live API.

### Suggested command sequence (Docker / CI parity)

```powershell
Set-Location d:\Hermes
python scripts/install_nimbusware.py --postgres-choice docker --seed-config
poetry run pytest tests -q -m "not integration"
.\scripts\run_integration_like_ci.ps1
# App profile (no Postgres): poetry run python scripts/e2e_smoke.py --profile app
# Full CI parity: poetry run python scripts/e2e_smoke.py --profile full
```

### Out of scope (v1 E2E)

- Multi-tenant load testing, production K8s deploy, full Ollama model pull in CI (too slow/heavy).
- Automating Windows `.exe` PostgreSQL install in GitHub-hosted runners (manual/`workflow_dispatch` on self-hosted only).
- Automating Windows `.exe` PostgreSQL install in GitHub-hosted runners (manual/`workflow_dispatch` on self-hosted only).
- Automating Windows `.exe` PostgreSQL install in GitHub-hosted runners (manual/`workflow_dispatch` on self-hosted only).
